## ADVANCED_LITIGATION_STRATEGIES(1).md
**Path:** `discovery\ADVANCED_LITIGATION_STRATEGIES(1).md`
**Time:** 18:44:07 | **Finds:** 5

- **Sanction**
  > #### Relief Requested  - Vacate all orders based on fraudulent evidence - Restore parenting time to July 17, 2024 order - Disqualify Judge McNeill - Sanction Emily Watson for fraud on the court - Award attorney fees and costs  #### Strategic Advantage  Fraud on the court is a ground for vacation tha

- **Sanctioned**
  > vexatious litigant finding - Limited Father's oral argument time - Muted Father during remote hearings  **Pattern 5: Unequal Treatment of Parties** - Sanctioned Father for disputed communication - Did not sanction Mother for documented withholding - Imposed parenting time restrictions on Father only

- **sanctions**
  > Find Emily Watson engaged in parental alienation constituting abuse - Modify custody to restrict Mother's ability to withhold parenting time - Impose sanctions on Mother for abuse - Award makeup parenting time - Award attorney fees and costs  #### Strategic Advantage  This claim shifts the focus fro

- **Contempt**
  > Evidence | Trial Court | Remove key basis for suspension | | 2 | Motion to Set Aside PPO | Trial Court | Eliminate fraudulent PPO | | 2 | Motion for Contempt | Trial Court | Sanction gatekeeping | | 2 | Criminal Complaint | Prosecutor | Criminal liability | | 3 | Judicial Tenure Complaint | JTC | Di

- **vexatious**
  > d convincing endangerment findings (MCL 722.27a(3) violation) - Rely on unauthenticated evidence (MRE 901 violation) - Impose $250 filing fee without vexatious litigant finding (MCR 2.002 violation)  #### Relief Requested  - Writ of mandamus directing trial court to restore parenting time - Writ of

- **Sanctions**
